CREATE TABLE `customreportsdefaults` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `countryid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `name` varchar(100) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `moduleid` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(25) DEFAULT NULL,  
  `updatedon` bigint(25) DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleteflag` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `defaultjson` mediumtext,  
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `defaultewaybills_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`countryid`) REFERENCES `country` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

update fieldparams set gstconfigtype=8 where fieldlabel in("Dispatch Document No","E-Way Bill No","E-Way Bill Date") and companyid in(select companyid from company where country=105);
update defaultcustomfields set gstconfigtype=8 where fieldlabel in("Dispatch Document No","E-Way Bill No","E-Way Bill Date");

#Nitesh Kumar 26th June 2018
update default_header set reftabledatacolumn='if(grorder.gstincluded="T",((grodetails.deliveredquantity*grodetails.rateincludegst)-(if(grodetails.discount IS NOT NULL,(select (if(grodetails.discountispercent=1,(grodetails.discount/100)*(rateincludegst*deliveredquantity),grodetails.discount))  ),0.0) )) ,((grodetails.deliveredquantity*grodetails.rate)-(if(grodetails.discount IS NOT NULL,(select (if(grodetails.discountispercent=1,(grodetails.discount/100)*(rate*deliveredquantity),grodetails.discount))  ),0.0) )+grodetails.rowtaxamount) ) ' where  id ='8d030d90-57dd-11e6-856d-c03fd5aad962';
